Let me know (see footer).</p>\n<p> </p>\n<h2>How to buy bitcoin using this list of exchanges?</h2>\n<p>Hopefully the list of bitcoin exchanges above will be of good use for how to trade bitcoins. Each outstanding site should have detailed instructions. From here, one can easily figure out how to buy bitcoin with credit card, paypal, cash, bank transfers. Once you have got some coins then it is a good idea to store them offline (not on an exchange). For cold storage check out the list of<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://bitcoin.org/en/choose-your-wallet\" target=\"_blank\"> available wallets</a>. When wanting buy or sell it is safer just to transfer in and out of your ‘cold’ wallet to the ‘hot’ online exchange. Remember that so long as an offline wallet’s keys have not been compromised, then those coins cannot be taken.</p>\n<p> </p>\n<h2>What is the best site to buy bitcoin in the above list?</h2>\n<p>It’s a tough question in my opinion. Each will have an upside compared to others. Check a few out and look up on forums to see what users are saying about the service provided, and which they think are the best sites to buy bitcoin easily. Localbitcoins.com is a really cool p2p bitcoin exchange for beginners wanting to buy for their first time. The service is all over the world, meaning you can use euros, pounds, yen, australian dollars, swiss francs, canadian dollars, krona, rubles, lira, rupees and so on. If you pay by physical cash then you get to meet the person in real life. Alternatively you can do a fast bank transfer and the site will hold your coins in escrow for you once it goes through. Obviously there are more simple ways to start off. Some like to buy with paypal, but not many leading bitcoin exchanges accept this because of chargebacks.</p>\n<p> </p>\n<h2>Which are the largest exchanges?</h2>\n<p>Generally the biggest bitcoin exchanges will be toward the top of the above list. For example OkCoin, GDAX, Btc-e, Coinbase (also the best usd bitcoin exchange) all represent large volume proportions. Daily volume varies, and therefore the world’s largest exchange vary each day. Go to <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://data.bitcoinity.org/markets/volume/24h?c=e&amp;t=b\" target=\"_blank\">bitcoinity</a> for a good list of all the top bitcoin exchange site and their proportional volumes. Some find this handy for arbitrage between markets.</p>\n<p> </p>\n<h2>What about the best cryptocurrency exchange?</h2>\n<p>Sadly, with the demise of Cryptsy there is a need for a new major first-rate cryptocurrency exchange (aka altcoins). Having many medium-sized cryptocurrency exchange sites is a better situation than having one large amazing option. Poloniex is the large amazing option. It’s a really good platform and the user-interface has gone through a complete redesign. Things feel smooth when using Poloniex. All big and small trading pairs are offered and it is now possible to do cryptocurrency margin trading on major altcoins. This is a cool feature, but use it with caution as leveraged trading has a certain risk factor. Keep in mind that some of the best bitcoin exchange sites also do altcoins. HitBTC, Bittrex, and CEX, are great options worth checking out. Some even offer short selling on major coins. You may also like to check the <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://coinmarketcap.com/\">market capitalizations</a> and compare them to others listed there.</p>\n<p> </p>\n<h2>Where to find the most secure bitcoin exchange?</h2>\n<p>This is an important question to ask. Yes, putting the words trustworthy bitcoin exchange in the same sentence seems like an oxymoron, especially when remembering the shiny days of MtGox (aka Empty-Gox). While the bitcoin protocol has never been hacked, many peripheral businesses have. Perhaps the best question to ask would be: which are the least secure bitcoin exchanges. Generally, those listed here are optimum and of good standing, but please proceed with caution. Remember never to leave more btc online than you can afford to loose.</p>\n<p> </p>\n<p style=\"margin: 15px 0 15px 0;\">Please come back to my blog and rate which ever finest site(s) you chose to buy BTC online. This helps future visitors immensely.</p><p style=\"margin: 15px 0 15px 0;\"> For in-depth discussion: listen to Andreas Antonopoulos on the <a href=\"https://soundcloud.com/mindtomatter\">LetsTalkBitcoin podcast</a>, and check out <a href=\"https://www.reddit.com/r/bitcoin\">r/bitcoin</a>.</p>\n\n<br>\n<h2>The best bitcoin exchanges in 2017:</h2>\n<br>\n<h3>Coinbase.com</h3>\n<p>Coinbase combine an attractive interface, a great site to get bitcoins with a debit card, and multiple online wallets for your digital currency. Over 4,800,000 users are signed up, including 45,000 merchants, and 9000 developer apps. Works well for European, American, &amp; Canadian customers. I’ve also written a comprehensive <a href=\"https://www.bestbitcoinexchange.io/coinbase-review/\">Coinbase review</a> for more detail.</p>\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Damn easy to use</p></li>\n\t<li><p>Lots of long-time customers</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>Online wallet available</p></li>\t\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Slightly more work needed when verifying account</p></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>Localbitcoins.com</h3>\n<p> Localbitcoins is quite a popular for p2p (person to person) transactions all over the world. Simply put, you interact directly with the guy selling to you. Out of all the bitcoin sites listed here, this is one of the first and most reputed. Escrow and dispute resolution is provided by the site.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Great way to meet people</p></li>\n\t<li><p>PayPal also available</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>No verification needed</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>Popular in most countries</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>May take longer to conclude transaction</p></li>\n\t<li><p>Risks associated with anonymous transactions</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>Some bank accounts have been suspended after receiving money</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>Bitstamp.net</h3>\n<p>Bitstamp are big in Europe and operate out of the United Kingdom. Good volumes are available for larger trades. Well received by people using SEPA and cards.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Card purchases available (visa mastercard)</p></li>\n\t<li><p>HQ Located in London</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>Good for large transactions</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Not available for many countries</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>Kraken.com</h3>\n<p>Kraken is becoming a reputed bitcoin broker, with many markets served. Europeans love it just as much as Americans because they work well through SEPA, have an easy verification process, and are very knowledgeable when it come to cryptography.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Cryptographic communications</p></li>\n\t<li><p>Cheapest rates</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>works well for Europeans and North America</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Site not as visually intuitive</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>CoinATMradar.com</h3>\n<p>CoinATMradar provide a global map of bitcoin ATMs. This allows you to use cash to buy in person at a physical machine. This is one of the most underrated means of purchasing with no verification of ID, and allows users to stay anonymous with over 869 ATMs srpead over each continent.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Find bitcoin locations near you</p></li>\n\t<li><p>No ID needed in some cases</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>Explains how a bitcoin atm works</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Not always possible to find a machine nearby</p></li>\n\t<li><p>You’ll have to leave your house!</p></li>\t\t\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>Paxful.com</h3>\n<p>Paxful get over 2 million monthly visits, with 50% originating from the USA. It’s a peer to peer Bitcoin marketplace connecting buyers with sellers similar to the one above. Over 150 payment methods can be used. Impressive.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Hundreds of payment methods</p></li>\n\t<li><p>p2p (person to person)</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Higher fees than elsewhere</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>Bitsquare.io</h3>\n<p>Bitsquare is not to be missed for the more technically advanced. A decentralized p2p platform that keeps you super safe. Over 60 crypocurrencies can be traded and you can even purcahse btc using a bank transfer, escrow, &amp; trusted 3rd parties.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Incredibly advanced (technologically)</p></li>\n\t<li><p>p2p <b>AND</b> decentralized</p></li>\t\n\t<li><p>Trusted escrow system for bank transfers</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>Advanced level of IT comprehension needed</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<br>\n<h3>GDAX.com</h3>\n<p>GDAX is great for technical traders and offers good liquidity. Deposits are in USD and can be processed just as rapidly as withdrawls. Aslo happens to be the best ethereum exchange for serious players in this space.</p>\n\n<div style=\"margin-left:30px;\">\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Pros</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>An integral part of the trusted Coinbase brand</p></li>\n\t<li><p>Optimized to be a serious trading site</p></li>\t\n</ul>\n<p class=\"procon\"><b>Cons</b></p>\n<ul>\n\t<li><p>More ID processing steps than on Chinese trading class=\"wc-comment-text\">It’s interesting to see how each exchange is taking a position (or not) relative to the two entrenched camps. On one side you have the majority of serious exchanges like Poloniex, Bitstamp, Kraken saying that the Bitcoin Core chain will always remain “BTC”. On the other side there are smaller exchanges like HitBTC who hint that BU is doing good for the ecosystem and we should all be happy. Then there are the neutral exchanges like Coinbase and Genimi who recently refused to sign a pro-BitcoinCore roadmap on what to do should there be a hard fork. It’s extremely insightful to see which CEO is taking which side and why. I believe that this is all merely just a phase. Bitcoin the technology and currency will continue to boom. It’s doing a really good job so far considering that governance is 100 percent decentralized. To buy btc with no ID verification it may be tricky these days as most exchanges are required by law to verify users identity. The recommended alternative is to use a person2person platform like LocalBitcoins where some sellers will not ask for any form of ID. Then there’s also the option of using a bitcoin ATM to buy anonymously. Here again, not all will sell without checking your ID.</p>\n<p>As for anonymous cryptocurrencies – that’s a very debatable question and not really within my scope of expertise, so I’ll leave it to others here to answer. question for some time now – so congratulations! Generally speaking, it is always best practise to store coins on an offline wallet over which only you have complete control. Good examples of offline desktop wallets include Multibit &amp; Armoury, or Mycelium for mobile phones (so not completely “offline”).</p>\n<p>That being said, online wallets are an excellent temporary storage system for quick and easy access. For this it’s best to store a limited amount of coins. I recommend this precaution for any online wallet system. Blockchain is definitely the most reputed online wallet and has millions of happy users.</p>\n<p>Blockchain have also recently introduced the ability for users to buy bitcoins with a credit card in most European countries (hence their addition in the ranking list above). Feel free to suggest any other similar service so that we can look into it further.</p>\n</div><div class=\"wc-comment-footer\"><div class=\"wc-footer-left\"><span class=\"wc-vote-link wc-up  wc_vote wc_not_clicked wc_tooltipster\"><i class=\"fa fa-thumbs-up fa-flip-horizontal wc-vote-img-up\"></i><span>Vote Up</span></span><span class=\"wc-vote-result\">0</span><span class=\"wc-vote-link wc-down  wc_vote wc_not_clicked wc_tooltipster\"><i class=\"fa fa-thumbs-down wc-vote-img-down\"></i><span>Vote Down</span></span>&nbsp;<span class=\"wc-reply-button wc-cta-button\" title=\"Reply\"><i class=\"fa fa-reply\" aria-hidden=\"true\"></i> Reply</span></div><div class=\"wc-footer-right\"><div class=\"wc-comment-date\"><i class=\"fa fa-clock-o\" aria-hidden=\"true\"></i>5 months 11 days ago</div><div class=\"wc-toggle wpdiscuz-hidden\"><i class=\"fa fa-chevron-up\" aria-hidden=\"true\" title=\"Hide Replies\"></i></div></div><div class=\"wpdiscuz_clear\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpdiscuz-comment-message\"></div><div id=\"wpdiscuz_form_anchor-27_26\" style=\"clear:both\"></div></div></div><div id=\"wc-comm-25_0\" class=\"wc-comment wc-blog-guest wc_comment_level-1\"><div class=\"wc-comment-left\"><img alt=\"Anonymous\" src=\"https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/8aba0b0e1ab2b4535e683bb58eee91e7?s=64&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g\" srcset=\"https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/8aba0b0e1ab2b4535e683bb58eee91e7?s=128&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x\" class=\"avatar avatar-64 photo\" height=\"64\" width=\"64\"><div class=\"wc-blog-guest wc-comment-label\"><span>Guest</span></div></div><div id=\"comment-25\" class=\"wc-comment-right \"><div class=\"wc-comment-header\"><div class=\"wc-comment-author\">Anonymous</div><div class=\"wc-comment-link\"><i class=\"fa fa-share-alt wc-share-link wpf-cta\" aria-hidden=\"true\" title=\"Share\"></i><span class=\"share_buttons_box\"><a class=\"wc_tw\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://twitter.com/home?status=A rather comprehensive list of sites where to buy bitcoin.
